btw, for those who are curious why Joey and natsuki were stirring their baths: Convection causes hot water to rise and cold water to sink. As a result, the water near the surface of the bath is extremely hot, to cool this down to a better temperature, one would stir the bath to mix the hot water and the colder water on the bottom.

I think those igloo houses are from a company called monolithic dot org here in the US.  They use a plastic dome in the shape of the building blown up with air, and spray plastic foam on the inside, lay rebar on the next layer in, then spray shotcrete (cement that can be sprayed out of an airgun,) on the innermost layer.  The result is the dome house that is earthquake resistant and hurricane resistant.  The foam has significant insulation factor, and can keep the inside fairly stable temperature-wise.  The company makes foam/concrete domes that can be an emergency shelter that can be moved quickly into place, be a mansion of several thousand square feet in floor area, to storage facilities for grain and explosives, to churches, to buildings housing indoor pools.   The hard bed and bathroom are the resort owner's choice. I wouldn't judge the dome based on that.
